toggle_county_commerce = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = show_county_commerce
			}
			remove_variable = show_county_commerce
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = toggle_county_commerce_t
				remove_variable = gui_t
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_tt
					add_to_global_variable_list = { 
						name = misc_chars
						target = this
					}
				}
				clear_variable_list = gui_t
				add_to_global_variable_list = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = toggle_county_commerce_t
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = show_county_commerce
				value = 1
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_food
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.county.var:trade_price_food
				}
				prev.county = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = gui_t
						value = 0
					}
					every_in_list = { 
						variable = trade_dat_food
						scope:gui_t = { 
							ordered_in_global_list = { 
								variable = misc_chars
								position = 0
								save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
								remove_list_global_variable = { 
									name = misc_chars
									target = this
								}
							}
							add_to_variable_list = { 
								name = gui_t
								target = scope:gui_tt
							}
						}
						scope:gui_tt = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_food
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_food
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									var:gui_tt < 0
								}
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_import
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_export
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
								}
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_cereal
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.county.var:trade_price_cereal
				}
				prev.county = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = gui_t
						value = 0
					}
					every_in_list = { 
						variable = trade_dat_cereal
						scope:gui_t = { 
							ordered_in_global_list = { 
								variable = misc_chars
								position = 0
								save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
								remove_list_global_variable = { 
									name = misc_chars
									target = this
								}
							}
							add_to_variable_list = { 
								name = gui_t
								target = scope:gui_tt
							}
						}
						scope:gui_tt = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_cereal
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_cereal
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									var:gui_tt < 0
								}
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_import
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_export
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
								}
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_salted
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.county.var:trade_price_salted
				}
				prev.county = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = gui_t
						value = 0
					}
					every_in_list = { 
						variable = trade_dat_salted
						scope:gui_t = { 
							ordered_in_global_list = { 
								variable = misc_chars
								position = 0
								save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
								remove_list_global_variable = { 
									name = misc_chars
									target = this
								}
							}
							add_to_variable_list = { 
								name = gui_t
								target = scope:gui_tt
							}
						}
						scope:gui_tt = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_salted
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_salted
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									var:gui_tt < 0
								}
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_import
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_export
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
								}
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_salt
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.county.var:trade_price_salt
				}
				prev.county = {

						value = 0
					}

							ordered_in_global_list = {

							}
						}

							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_salt
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_salt
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									var:gui_tt < 0
								}
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_import
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_export
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
								}
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_mud
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.county.var:trade_price_mud
				}
				prev.county = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = gui_t
						value = 0
					}
					every_in_list = { 
						variable = trade_dat_mud
						scope:gui_t = { 
							ordered_in_global_list = {

								position = 0

								name = gui_t
								target = scope:gui_tt
							}
						}
						scope:gui_tt = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_mud
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_mud
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									var:gui_tt < 0
								}
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_import
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt

										name = gui_tt

									give_nickname = gui_export

										name = gui_tt

								save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
								remove_list_global_variable = { 
									name = misc_chars
									target = this
								}
							}
							add_to_variable_list = { 
								name = gui_t
								target = scope:gui_tt
							}
						}
						scope:gui_tt = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_tools
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_tools
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									var:gui_tt < 0
								}
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_import
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_export
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
								}
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_county_commerce_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_armaments
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.county.var:trade_price_armaments
				}
				prev.county = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = gui_t
						value = 0
					}
					every_in_list = { 
						variable = trade_dat_armaments
						scope:gui_t = { 
							ordered_in_global_list = { 
								variable = misc_chars
								position = 0
								save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
								remove_list_global_variable = { 
									name = misc_chars
									target = this
								}
							}
							add_to_variable_list = { 
								name = gui_t
								target = scope:gui_tt
							}
						}
						scope:gui_tt = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_armaments
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_armaments
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									var:gui_tt < 0
								}
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_import
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								scope:gui_tt = { 
									give_nickname = gui_export
									set_variable = { 
										name = gui_tt
										value = prev.var:gui_tt
									}
								}
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			county = { 
				remove_variable = gui_t
				remove_variable = gui_tt
			}
		}
	}
}
close_county_commerce = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = show_county_commerce
			}
			remove_variable = show_county_commerce
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = toggle_county_commerce_t
				remove_variable = gui_t
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_tt
					add_to_global_variable_list = { 
						name = misc_chars
						target = this
					}
				}
				clear_variable_list = gui_t
				add_to_global_variable_list = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = toggle_county_commerce_t
		}
	}
}
toggle_province_economy = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = show_province_economy
			}
			remove_variable = show_province_economy
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = toggle_province_economy_t
				remove_variable = gui_t
				remove_variable = gui_tt
				remove_variable = gui_ttt
				remove_variable = gui_tttt
				add_to_global_variable_list = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = toggle_province_economy_t
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = show_province_economy
				value = 1
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_province_economy_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_food
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.var:prod_has_food
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_tt
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_ttt
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_tttt
					value = 0
				}
				prev = { 
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = pop_calorie_food
							var:pop_calorie_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								add = prev.var:pop_calorie_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = pop_calorie_actual_food
							var:pop_calorie_actual_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_ttt
								add = prev.var:pop_calorie_actual_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = pop_nutrient_food
							var:pop_nutrient_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								add = prev.var:pop_nutrient_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = pop_nutrient_actual_food
							var:pop_nutrient_actual_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_ttt
								add = prev.var:pop_nutrient_actual_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = pop_comfort_food
							var:pop_comfort_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								add = prev.var:pop_comfort_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = pop_comfort_actual_food
							var:pop_comfort_actual_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_ttt
								add = prev.var:pop_comfort_actual_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = pop_luxury_food
							var:pop_luxury_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								add = prev.var:pop_luxury_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = pop_luxury_actual_food
							var:pop_luxury_actual_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_ttt
								add = prev.var:pop_luxury_actual_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = mil_supply_food
							var:mil_supply_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								add = prev.var:mil_supply_food
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							has_variable = mil_supply_in_food
							var:mil_supply_in_food > 0
						}
						prev = { 
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_ttt
								add = prev.var:mil_supply_in_food
							}
						}
					}
					every_in_list = {

								var:prod_sply_old_food > 0

								}
							}

								change_variable = {

									add = prev.var:prod_in_old_food
								}

						}
					}
					every_in_list = {

						prev = {

				position = 0

				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this

			}

				target = scope:gui_t

					value = 0

close_province_economy = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = show_province_economy
			}
			remove_variable = show_province_economy
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = toggle_province_economy_t
				remove_variable = gui_t
				remove_variable = gui_tt
				remove_variable = gui_ttt
				remove_variable = gui_tttt
				add_to_global_variable_list = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = toggle_province_economy_t
		}
	}
}
toggle_province_townhall = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = show_province_townhall
			}
			remove_variable = show_province_townhall
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = toggle_province_townhall_t
				remove_variable = gui_t
				remove_variable = gui_farm
				remove_variable = gui_pasture
				remove_variable = gui_forest
				remove_variable = gui_extraction
				remove_variable = gui_workshop
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_t
					add_to_global_variable_list = { 
						name = misc_chars
						target = this
					}
				}
				clear_variable_list = gui_t
				add_to_global_variable_list = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = toggle_province_townhall_t
		}
		else = { 
			set_variable = { 
				name = show_province_townhall
				value = 1
			}
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = prod_instances
				prev = { 
					ordered_in_global_list = { 
						variable = misc_chars
						position = 0
						save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
						remove_list_global_variable = { 
							name = misc_chars
							target = this
						}
					}
					add_to_variable_list = { 
						name = toggle_province_townhall_t
						target = scope:gui_t
					}
				}
				if = { 
					limit = { 
						var:prod_template = global_var:vegetables
					}
					scope:gui_t = { 
						give_nickname = gui_ind_vegetables
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							global_var:vegetables = { 
								has_variable = prod_land_farm
							}
						}
						scope:gui_t = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_farm
								value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							global_var:vegetables = { 
								has_variable = prod_land_pasture
							}
						}
						scope:gui_t = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_pasture
								value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							global_var:vegetables = { 
								has_variable = prod_land_forest
							}
						}
						scope:gui_t = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_forest

							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = {

								has_variable = prod_land_extraction
							}
						}
						scope:gui_t = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_extraction
								value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					if = { 
						limit = { 
							global_var:vegetables = { 
								has_variable = prod_land_workshop
							}
						}
						scope:gui_t = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_workshop
								value = 1
							}
						}
					}
					scope:gui_t = { 
						set_variable = { 
							name = gui_t
							value = prev
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { 
								prev = { 
									has_variable = prod_dmnd_old_food
								}
							}
							ordered_in_global_list = { 
								variable = misc_chars
								position = 0
								save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
								remove_list_global_variable = { 
									name = misc_chars
									target = this
								}
							}
							add_to_variable_list = {

							prev = {

	scope = province
	is_shown = {

	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = show_province_townhall
			}
			remove_variable = show_province_townhall
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = toggle_province_townhall_t
				remove_variable = gui_t
				remove_variable = gui_farm
				remove_variable = gui_pasture
				remove_variable = gui_forest
				remove_variable = gui_extraction
				remove_variable = gui_workshop
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_t
					add_to_global_variable_list = { 
						name = misc_chars
						target = this
					}
				}
				clear_variable_list = gui_t
				add_to_global_variable_list = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = toggle_province_townhall_t
		}
	}
}
toggle_province_merchant = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = show_province_merchant
			}
			remove_variable = show_province_merchant
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = toggle_province_merchant_t
				remove_variable = gui_t
				remove_variable = gui_tt
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_tt
					remove_variable = gui_ttt
					add_to_global_variable_list = { 
						name = misc_chars
						target = this
					}
				}
				clear_variable_list = gui_t
				add_to_global_variable_list = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = toggle_province_merchant_t
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = trade_merchant
			}
			set_variable = { 
				name = show_province_merchant
				value = 1
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_province_merchant_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_food
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.var:trade_merchant.var:trade_price_food
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_tt
					value = prev.var:trade_merchant.var:trade_has_food
				}
				prev.var:trade_merchant = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = gui_t
						value = 0
					}
					every_in_list = { 
						variable = trade_dat_food
						ordered_in_global_list = { 
							variable = misc_chars
							position = 0
							save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
							remove_list_global_variable = { 
								name = misc_chars
								target = this
							}
						}
						scope:gui_t = { 
							add_to_variable_list = { 
								name = gui_t
								target = scope:gui_tt
							}
						}
						scope:gui_tt = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { 
								has_variable = trade_merchant
							}
							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_tt
									value = 1
								}
							}
						}
						else_if = { 
							limit = { 
								has_variable = pop_total
							}
							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_tt
									value = 2
								}
							}
						}
						else = { 
							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_tt
									value = 3
								}
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_food
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_food
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_ttt
									value = prev.var:gui_tt
								}
								if = { 
									limit = { 
										var:gui_ttt < 0
									}
									give_nickname = gui_import
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_ttt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}
								else = { 
									give_nickname = gui_export
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_province_merchant_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}
			scope:gui_t = { 
				give_nickname = gui_cereal
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.var:trade_merchant.var:trade_price_cereal
				}
				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_tt
					value = prev.var:trade_merchant.var:trade_has_cereal
				}
				prev.var:trade_merchant = { 
					set_variable = { 
						name = gui_t
						value = 0
					}
					every_in_list = { 
						variable = trade_dat_cereal
						ordered_in_global_list = { 
							variable = misc_chars
							position = 0
							save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
							remove_list_global_variable = { 
								name = misc_chars
								target = this
							}
						}
						scope:gui_t = { 
							add_to_variable_list = { 
								name = gui_t
								target = scope:gui_tt
							}
						}
						scope:gui_tt = { 
							set_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								value = prev
							}
						}
						if = { 
							limit = { 
								has_variable = trade_merchant
							}
							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_tt
									value = 1
								}
							}
						}
						else_if = { 
							limit = { 
								has_variable = pop_total
							}
							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_tt
									value = 2
								}
							}
						}
						else = { 
							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_tt
									value = 3
								}
							}
						}
						prev = { 
							set_global_variable = { 
								name = array_get_t
								value = var:gui_t
							}
							if = { 
								limit = { 
									OR = { 
										NOT = { 
											has_global_variable = array_get_t
										}
										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_cereal
									position = 0
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = { 
								ordered_in_list = { 
									variable = array_trade_dat_cereal
									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = { 
											name = gui_tt
											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_tt
								divide = 10
							}
							remove_global_variable = array_get_t
							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_ttt
									value = prev.var:gui_tt
								}
								if = { 
									limit = { 
										var:gui_ttt < 0
									}
									give_nickname = gui_import
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_ttt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}
								else = { 
									give_nickname = gui_export
								}
							}
							change_variable = { 
								name = gui_t
								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ordered_in_global_list = { 
				variable = misc_chars
				position = 0
				save_temporary_scope_as = gui_t
				remove_list_global_variable = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			add_to_variable_list = { 
				name = toggle_province_merchant_t
				target = scope:gui_t
			}

				set_variable = { 
					name = gui_t
					value = prev.var:trade_merchant.var:trade_price_salted
				}
				set_variable = {

					value = prev.var:trade_merchant.var:trade_has_salted

							position = 0
							save_temporary_scope_as = gui_tt
							remove_list_global_variable = {

										global_var:array_get_t = 0
									}
								}

									position = 0

											value = prev
										}
									}
								}
							}
							else = {

									position = global_var:array_get_t.compare_value
									prev = { 
										set_variable = {

											value = prev
										}
									}
								}

								divide = 10
							}

							scope:gui_tt = { 
								set_variable = { 
									name = gui_ttt
									value = prev.var:gui_tt
								}

									limit = { 
										var:gui_ttt < 0
									}
									give_nickname = gui_import
									change_variable = { 
										name = gui_ttt
										multiply = -1
									}
								}

									give_nickname = gui_export
								}
							}

								add = 1
							}

					}
				}

									}

							}
							else = {

									variable = array_trade_dat_armaments

								add = 1
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			var:trade_merchant = { 
				remove_variable = gui_t
				remove_variable = gui_tt
			}
		}
	}
}
close_province_merchant = { 
	scope = province
	is_shown = { 
		always = yes
	}
	is_valid = { 
		always = yes
	}
	effect = { 
		if = { 
			limit = { 
				has_variable = show_province_merchant
			}
			remove_variable = show_province_merchant
			every_in_list = { 
				variable = toggle_province_merchant_t
				remove_variable = gui_t
				remove_variable = gui_tt
				remove_variable = gui_ttt
				every_in_list = { 
					variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_t
					remove_variable = gui_tt
					add_to_global_variable_list = { 
						name = misc_chars
						target = this
					}
				}
				clear_variable_list = gui_t
				add_to_global_variable_list = { 
					name = misc_chars
					target = this
				}
			}
			clear_variable_list = toggle_province_merchant_t
		}
	}
}
